# Star Citizen Ship Default Loadouts Catalog

This document lists the default equipped components and weapons for each player-ownable ship, extracted from the game data records database.

- [Aegis Dynamics](#aegis-dynamics)
- [Anvil Aerospace](#anvil-aerospace)
- [Argo Astronautics](#argo-astronautics)
- [Banu](#banu)

- [Esperia](#esperia)
